Out Of Edward Jones Transaction Test

  1 To 10 Seconds (Duration)   Priority-4   Platform1-Regression   DB-Test-Data   Ach-Out-Of-Flow MICROSOFTEDGE

Card 2 - Select, Search, Sort for Edward Jones account for 'OUT OF' flow (ATMT-15235, ATMT-18057, ATMT-20988)
Steps Screenshots Outcome
Retrieve random data from DB2: EJ account from relationship with many accounts, ownership ruleID=309, branch=BR_4454
SUCCESS 5s 790ms
Retrieve data from DB2: EJ account from relationship with many accounts, ownership ruleID=309, branch=BR_4454, program code SELECT

SQL query  Copy 

select
acct.ACCT_ID, acct.CUST_NO,
rlt.RLTSHP_ID AS RLTSHP_ID,
acct_svc.ACCT_SVC_TY_CD, acct_svc.ACCT_SVC_STAT_CD, acct.ACCT_OWN_RULE_ID,
sub_acc.br_no

from PROD.RLTSHP_13120 rlt
join PROD.ACCT_FUNC_GRP_DTL_13088 grp on rlt.ACCT_FUNC_GRP_ID = grp.ACCT_FUNC_GRP_ID
join PROD.ACCOUNT_12280 as acct on grp.ACCT_ID = acct.ACCT_ID
join PROD.SUB_ACCOUNT_12512 as sub_acc on sub_acc.ACCT_ID=acct.ACCT_ID
join PROD.SUBACCT_SVC_12569 as acct_svc on acct_svc.ACCT_ID=acct.ACCT_ID

where
acct.TAX_RPT_CTRY_CD='US'
and acct.LGCL_DEL_DA is null
and acct.ACCT_CLS_DA is  null
and acct.ACCT_OWN_RULE_ID = 309
and sub_acc.br_no  = 4454
 and acct_svc.ACCT_SVC_STAT_CD in ('A', 'C')
 and rlt.RLTSHP_ID in (
select rlt.RLTSHP_ID
  from PROD.RLTSHP_13120 rlt
  join PROD.ACCT_FUNC_GRP_DTL_13088 grp on rlt.ACCT_FUNC_GRP_ID = grp.ACCT_FUNC_GRP_ID
  join PROD.ACCOUNT_12280 as acct on grp.ACCT_ID = acct.ACCT_ID
  join PROD.SUB_ACCOUNT_12512 as sub_acc on sub_acc.ACCT_ID=acct.ACCT_ID
  join PROD.SUBACCT_SVC_12569 as acct_svc on acct_svc.ACCT_ID=acct.ACCT_ID

  where
    acct.TAX_RPT_CTRY_CD='US'
    and acct.LGCL_DEL_DA is null
    and acct.ACCT_CLS_DA is null
    and sub_acc.br_no  = 4454

 group by rlt.RLTSHP_ID
 having count(acct.ACCT_ID)>4
)
 and acct_svc.ACCT_SVC_TY_CD in ('SE')
 

 and sub_acc.acct_id not in
 (               select a.acct_id
                 from
                     PROD.ACCOUNT_12280 a
                     left outer join PROD.acct_rst_10214 v on v.account_no= a.cust_no
                     inner join PROD.ACCT_OWN_RUL_12520 acc_own_rule on acc_own_rule.ACCT_OWN_RULE_ID =  a.ACCT_OWN_RULE_ID
                     inner join PROD.OWN_CLASS_12680 cls on  acc_own_rule.ACCT_OWN_RULE_ID =  cls.ACCT_OWN_RULE_ID
                     inner join PROD.SUB_ACCOUNT_12512 as sub_acc on sub_acc.ACCT_ID=a.ACCT_ID
                 where
                     v.rst_rsn_cd is not null
                     and v.rst_rsn_cd in ( 'AUTH', 'DOCU', 'WARN', 'CIPR', 'COPD', 'CO', 'RISK', 'SSN', 'FTRN', '72T', 'MISC', 'MAIL', 'FOR', 'FOR2', 'R471', 'R407','DEATH' )
                     and a.LGCL_DEL_DA is null
                     and a.ACCT_CLS_DA is null
                     and a.ACCT_OWN_RULE_ID = 309
                     and sub_acc.br_no  = 4454
                     and v.RST_START_DA<'2025-10-06'
 )

FETCH FIRST 500 ROWS ONLY

SUCCESS 5s 207ms
Get sub accounts for EJ account with ID 145219316

SQL query  Copy 

select
        sub_acc.ACCT_ID as ACCT_ID,
        count(distinct sub_acc_type1.ACCT_ID) as COUNT_CASH,
        count(distinct sub_acc_type2.ACCT_ID) as COUNT_MARGIN,
        count(distinct sub_acc_type4.ACCT_ID) as COUNT_LOAN

from PROD.SUB_ACCOUNT_12512 as sub_acc
        left outer join PROD.SUBACCT_TYPE_12528 as sub_acc_type1 on (sub_acc.ACCT_ID = sub_acc_type1.ACCT_ID and sub_acc_type1.ACCT_TY_CD = 1) --cash
        left outer join PROD.SUBACCT_TYPE_12528 as sub_acc_type2 on (sub_acc.ACCT_ID = sub_acc_type2.ACCT_ID and sub_acc_type2.ACCT_TY_CD = 2) --margin
        left outer join PROD.SUBACCT_TYPE_12528 as sub_acc_type4 on (sub_acc.ACCT_ID = sub_acc_type4.ACCT_ID and sub_acc_type4.ACCT_TY_CD = 4) --loan

where sub_acc.acct_ID=145219316
group by sub_acc.ACCT_ID

SQL result  Copy 

{COUNT_CASH=1, ACCT_ID=145219316, COUNT_LOAN=1, COUNT_MARGIN=1}

Subaccounts  Copy 

{CASH=true, MARGIN=true, LOAN=true}
